📌 Trip Summary

📑 On this page: 📋 Summary 🌍 Fun Facts 🏷️ Legend 🗺️ Map 🌟 Itinerary

📋 Summary — Crew and Vehicle

👨‍👩‍👧‍👦 Crew: 2 adults + 2 children (8 and 6 years old)

🚐 Vehicle: self-sufficient camper van (LiFePo4 + 5 kg gas cylinder)

📅 Period: 26/06/2026 (afternoon) → 18/08/2026 (evening) — 54 days

🛣️ Total km: ~12,320 km

🌑 Key event: 🌒 Total Solar Eclipse — 12/08/2026, area Palencia (🇪🇸), totality ~8:29 pm local, Sun at ~11° above West horizon

🎯 Trip focus: nature, parks and museums for children, scenic roads (🛣️), total eclipse, thermal experiences, fishing 🎣, trekking 🥾

🌍 Fun Facts — Geographic Data

🌍 Countries crossed: 🇮🇹 🇦🇹 🇨🇿 🇵🇱 🇱🇹 🇱🇻 🇪🇪 🇫🇮 🇳🇴 🇩🇰 🇩🇪 🇫🇷 🇪🇸 (13)

📍 Geographic extremes: North → Tromsø / Senja (🇳🇴) · South → Palencia (🇪🇸)

🌊 Seas touched: Baltic Sea · Arctic Ocean · Norwegian Sea · Atlantic · Mediterranean Sea

🛣️ Iconic scenic roads (🛣️): Via Baltica · Punkaharju Ridge · Senja NTR · Andøya NTR · Lofoten (E10) NTR · Helgelandskysten · Atlantic Road · Geiranger–Trollstigen NTR · Hardanger NTR · Jæren NTR + Nordsjøvegen · Storebælt Bridge · Marguerite Route · Basque Corniche · Desfiladero de la Hermida

📅 Itinerary — Day by Day

📑 On this page: D0–D10 Central Europe D11–D15 Finland/Tromsø D16–D23 Senja/Lofoten D24–D33 Southern Norway D33–D39 Denmark D40–D42 France D43–D49 Spain D50–D53 Return ☀️ Weather 🗺️ Alternatives ☔ Rain Plan 🎉 Festivals and Events

🛣️ Details — Day by Day

Each block includes: route, tolls/ferries, weather, POI, alternatives, fishing 🎣 where possible, Maps keywords.

D0 · 26/06 · Selvazzano → Leoben 🇮🇹→🇦🇹

350 km · 3h 30m · Tolls A4+A23 ~€15 + digital AT vignette €12.80 (10 days)

☀️ 25°C / 14°C · Good weather · 16h daylight

🚗 Departure in the afternoon, arrival evening in Leoben — where it all began 🌒 This is where we saw our first total solar eclipse (August 11, 1999). The trip begins and ends with an eclipse! 🌭 Leoben street food: Gasthäuser in Hauptplatz — Styrian cuisine: Brettljause (cold cuts and cheese board) ~€10-14, Backhendl (Styrian fried chicken) ~€12, Steirischer Schweinsbraten (roast pork) ~€11. Everything drizzled with the famous Kürbiskernöl (pumpkin seed oil). Beer: Gösser Bräu — Gösser beer was born here!

👶 Kids: 1. Leopark (St. Michael bei Leoben): Indoor playground with activities for all ages. 2. Kunsthalle Leoben: Interactive museum for children aged 6-14, a museum within a museum!

📋 Practical Info

🅿️ Accommodation: Campingclub Hinterberg (Hinterbergstr. 47, Leoben) - 📍 Maps From €25/night (all inclusive). Children under 15 free, pets free. Family-run, quiet. Check-in 7AM-9PM.

⛽ Fuel: Main fuel station chains in Austria include OMV, BP, Shell, and Eni. No significant remote stretches without fuel on this highway route. Approximate diesel price: €1.88-1.95/L (AT).

🛣️ Tolls: In Italy, standard highway tolls apply (approx. €15-20 from Padova to the border). In Austria, a vignette is mandatory for vehicles up to 3.5 tons (approx. €12.80 for 10 days). If the camper is over 3.5 tons, a GO-Box is required for mileage-based tolls.

⏰ Timing: Suggested departure from Selvazzano (Padova) in the early afternoon (e.g., 14:00). The drive takes about 3.5 hours (approx. 350 km via A4+A23+S6). Expected arrival in Leoben around 17:30. This allows time to settle at the campsite and take a stroll through the beautiful Hauptplatz before dinner.

🛒 Supermarkets: Interspar at LCS Leoben City Shopping — 📍 Maps; Merkur Markt (Pichlmayergasse 16) — 📍 Maps

🧺 Laundry: Self-service laundry available at Campingclub Hinterberg.

💧 Water/Dump: Campingclub Hinterberg offers fresh water fill and grey/black water dump stations for guests.

🏥 Safety: Nearest hospital: LKH Hochsteiermark Leoben (regional state hospital) — 📍 Maps. Emergency numbers: 144 (Ambulance), 133 (Police), 122 (Fire), 112 (European Emergency). Note: Austrian vignette required on motorways.

💰 Daily budget: €100-140

Tolls: Italian highway A4+A23 (~€15) + digital Austrian vignette to buy on asfinag.at (€12.80 for 10 days, 2026 price).

🛴 Scooters: Leoben city center — compact old town, ideal for an evening stroll → see rentals

Maps: 📍 Leoben

👶 Kids: 1. Schönbrunn Palace and Gardens (including the Labyrinth and Gloriette) - great for kids to explore. 2. Vienna Zoo (Schönbrunner Tiergarten) - the oldest zoo in the world, very kid-friendly. 3. Prater Amusement Park - features the famous Giant Ferris Wheel and many rides.

📋 Practical Info

🅿️ Accommodation: 1. Reisemobilstellplatz Wien (Perfektastraße 49-53, 1230 Wien). 📍 Maps Price: ~€27-30/night. Features: electricity, water, disposal, open 24h. 2. MICAMPA Wien Wienerwald (Hüttelbergstr. 80, 1140 Wien). Features: near Vienna Woods, hiking trails, family-friendly.

⛽ Fuel: Main fuel station chains in Austria include OMV, BP, Shell, and Eni. No major remote stretches without fuel on the S6/A2 motorway from Leoben to Vienna. Approximate diesel price: €1.88 - €1.95 per liter.

🛣️ Tolls: A vignette is mandatory for vehicles up to 3.5 tons on Austrian motorways. A 1-day digital vignette costs €8.60. For vehicles over 3.5 tons, a GO-Box is required for mileage-based tolls.

⏰ Timing: Suggest departing Leoben around 09:00. The drive to Vienna is about 1h 45m (approx. 150 km via S6/A2). Expected arrival in Vienna around 11:00, allowing plenty of time for sightseeing. Afternoon can be spent setting up at the campsite and visiting a nearby attraction like Schönbrunn Palace (check closing times, usually around 17:00-17:30).

🛒 Supermarkets: Main supermarket chains in Austria: Spar (Interspar, Eurospar), Billa (Billa Plus), Hofer (discount), and Lidl. You will find many of these along the route and near the campsites in Vienna.

🧺 Laundry: Green & Clean (self-service laundromat chain in Vienna, e.g., near U-Bahn stations, approx. €15 per load). Verify locally for the closest branch to your campsite.

💧 Water/Dump: Available at Reisemobilstellplatz Wien (included in pitch price) and Camping Wien West. Dedicated service points for fresh water fill and grey/black water dump are provided at these campsites.

🏥 Safety: Nearest major hospital in Vienna: Vienna General Hospital (AKH Wien). Emergency numbers in Austria: European emergency 112, Ambulance/Rescue 144, Police 133, Fire 122. Warning: Ensure vignette is purchased before entering motorways to avoid heavy fines.

💰 Daily budget: €130-160

D1 · 27/06 · Leoben → Vienna 🇦🇹

150 km · 1h 45m · AT vignette (already active)

☀️ 25°C / 15°C · Possible afternoon thunderstorms · 16h daylight

🛣️ ‍👩‍👧‍👦 ⭐ Prater — Ferris wheel + vintage rides 🏛️ Haus der Musik — conduct the Vienna Philharmonic (interactive!) 🌭 Vienna street food: Bitzinger's Würstelstand (Albertinaplatz, behind the Opera) — Käsekrainer (cheese sausage) ~€5-7, Viennese institution! Or falafel wrap at Naschmarkt ~€5-8. Market: Naschmarkt (Wienzeile) — stalls from all over the world, spices, sweets, olives. Mon-Sat. ➕ alt: Therme Wien Oberlaa (evening) → see ♨️ details ➕ alt: Schönbrunn + Zoo (if arriving early)

🛴 Scooters: Vienna Ringstrasse, Prater, Donauinsel — all flat, excellent bike lanes → see rentals

Maps: 📍 Prater Wien

👶 Kids: To break up the long 7-8 hour drive, stop in Brno (Czech Republic) to visit the VIDA! Science Centre, which is highly interactive and great for kids, or find a local park for a picnic. Once in Warsaw, the Copernicus Science Centre is a fantastic kid-friendly activity.

📋 Practical Info

🅿️ Accommodation: 1. Camping WOK (Warsaw) - 📍 Maps Price: ~€35/night (approx 150 PLN). Features: electricity, water, WiFi, playground, very clean facilities, highly recommended for families.
2. Camping Majawa (Warsaw) - 📍 Maps Price: ~€28/night. Features: basic amenities, closer to the city center but less resort-like than WOK.

⛽ Fuel: Czech Republic: Benzina (Orlen), MOL, OMV. Poland: Orlen, BP, Shell, Lotos. There are no remote stretches without fuel on this major highway route. Approximate diesel price: €1.65 - €1.72 per liter (CZ) / €1.55 - €1.62 per liter (PL).

🛣️ Tolls: Austria: Vignette required (10-day ~€11.50, likely already purchased on G1). Czech Republic: Electronic vignette required for vehicles <3.5t (10-day ~€11 / 270 CZK). Poland: The route via A1/S8 is mostly toll-free for vehicles <3.5t. Note: If the camper van is >3.5t, electronic toll boxes (Myto CZ in Czechia and e-TOLL in Poland) are mandatory and costs will be significantly higher based on per-km rates.

⏰ Timing: Suggested departure from Vienna: 08:00. The drive is long (~680 km, 7-8 hours pure driving). Plan a 2-hour lunch and play break in Brno around 10:00-12:00. Expected arrival at the Warsaw campsite: 17:00-18:00.

🛒 Supermarkets: Czech Republic: Albert, Tesco, Kaufland. Poland: Biedronka, Lidl, Auchan, Kaufland. There are numerous large supermarkets along the route and very close to the campsites in Warsaw for easy restocking.

🧺 Laundry: Camping WOK in Warsaw has excellent on-site self-service laundry facilities (washing machines and dryers available for a small token fee).

💧 Water/Dump: Fresh water fill and grey/black water dump are available at Camping WOK. Major Orlen service stations along the Polish A1 and S8 highways also frequently offer dedicated camper service points for water and dumping.

🏥 Safety: Emergency number: 112 (valid across Austria, Czech Republic, and Poland). Nearest hospital in Warsaw: Children's Clinical Hospital UCC MUW (Dziecięcy Szpital Kliniczny). Warning: Watch out for heavy truck traffic and ongoing roadworks on the A1/S8 corridors in Poland.

💰 Daily budget: €180-210

D2 · 28/06 · Vienna → Warsaw 🇦🇹→🇨🇿→🇵🇱

670 km · 7h 30m · CZ vignette 310 CZK/~€13 (10 days) + PL tolls ~€15-20

☀️ 23°C / 13°C · Afternoon thunderstorms · 17h daylight

⚠️ BALTIC MARATHON START (D2–D5): 1,700 km in 4 days. Start at 5:00-6:00 — kids sleep first 3-4h. Arrival at destination by lunch → see risks 🏛️ Stop Brno: Villa Tugendhat (Unesco, 30 min) — ⚠️ CLOSED MONDAY + mandatory reservation on tugendhat.eu (max 16 pax/turn, quick sell-out!) 🌲 ‍👩‍👧‍👦 Evening Warsaw: Multimedia Fountains — open fountain park (interactive water jets for children). ⚠️ The evening multimedia show (lights+laser+music) is only Fri and Sat — D2 = Sunday, so no evening show. The park is still nice by day! ➕ alt evening: Copernicus Science Centre (open Sun, interactive, perfect for kids 6-8, €12/pax) + illuminated Old Town walk ➕ alt: Olomouc instead of Brno (fewer tourists) 🌭 Warsaw street food: Zapiekanki (toasted baguettes) at Plac Nowy or kiosks on the Vistula ~€3-4. Obwarzanki (bread rings) from street vendors ~€1. Bar Mleczny Familijny (Nowy Świat 39) — pierogi ~€3, barszcz ~€1.50. Market: Hala Mirowska (Pl. Mirowski) — fresh products, bread, cold cuts. Mon-Sat. 🛍️ Flea market: Bazar na Kole (Obozowa 99) — Warsaw's biggest flea market! Antiques, Soviet memorabilia, vinyl records, vintage furniture. Sun morning 6:00-14:00 — 📍 Maps

Tolls: Czech Republic digital vignette 310 CZK (~€13) for 10 days on edalnice.cz. Poland: highway tolls A1/A2/A4 managed by concessionaires (~€15-20 total, cash or card payment at toll booths).

🛴 Scooters: Warsaw historic center wide and pedestrian, Vistula riverbank → see rentals

Maps: 📍 Multimedia Fountain Warsaw

👶 Kids: 1. Toys Museum (Žaislų muziejus) in Vilnius Old Town - an edutainment center where children can play with replicas of historical toys. 2. Gediminas Castle Tower - fun to take the funicular up the hill for great views of the city.

📋 Practical Info

🅿️ Accommodation: Vilnius City Campsite (Laisvės pr. 5, Vilnius LT 04215). 📍 Maps Price: ~€30 per night (Motorhome pitch €15 + Adult €9 + Child €4). Features: Electricity (10A), fresh water, waste disposal, Wi-Fi, showers, washing machine, near Litexpo Exhibition Center.

⛽ Fuel: Main fuel chains in Poland: Orlen, Lotos, BP. Main chains in Lithuania: Circle K, Viada, Neste. Diesel price in Poland: ~€1.49/L. Diesel price in Lithuania: ~€1.61/L. No major remote stretches without fuel on this main route (E67/Via Baltica).

🛣️ Tolls: In Poland, camper vans with a GVM over 3.5t are subject to the e-TOLL system on national roads and highways. In Lithuania, tolls are charged on vehicles over 3.5 tonnes, but passenger camper vans (M1 category) are generally exempt from the vignette requirement. Approximate cost: €15-25 for the Polish section depending on the exact route and vehicle weight.

⏰ Timing: Suggest departing Warsaw around 08:00. The drive is about 470 km and takes roughly 6-7 hours in a camper van. Expected arrival in Vilnius around 15:00-16:00. Note: Lithuania is 1 hour ahead of Poland (EET vs CET), so you lose an hour.

🛒 Supermarkets: Main supermarket chains in Lithuania: Maxima, IKI, Rimi, Lidl. There is an IKI supermarket along the route (e.g., in Garliava) and supermarkets near the Vilnius City Campsite (approx. 0.45 km away).

🧺 Laundry: Speed Queen Self-Service Laundry (Laundromat) in Žirmūnai, Verkių Street 31 C (Outlet Park), open 05:00 - 02:00. Also Londris self-service laundromats available in Vilnius.

💧 Water/Dump: Vilnius City Campsite offers fresh water refill, grey water disposal, and chemical toilet disposal on-site.

🏥 Safety: Nearest hospital for adults: Republican Vilnius University Hospital (Šiltnamių st. 29, Vilnius) or Santaros Clinics (Santariškių g. 2). Emergency number: 112. Warnings: Watch out for heavy agricultural vehicles and unlit bicycles/vehicles in rural areas.

💰 Daily budget: €120-150

D3 · 29/06 · Warsaw → Vilnius 🇵🇱→🇱🇹

470 km · 6h 30m · Via S-61/E67 (Białystok–Suwałki) · Free (no tolls)

☀️ 22°C / 12°C · Good weather · 17h 30m daylight

🌲 Bernardinai Garden — water playground 🏛️ Uzupis — "independent republic" of artists 🌭 Vilnius street food: Kibinai (filled pastries, Karaite specialty) ~€3 — sold everywhere downtown. Kepta Duona (fried garlic bread) from kiosks ~€3-4. To sit down: Forto Dvaras (Pilies g. 16) — cepelinai ~€6. Market: Halės Turgus (Pylimo g. 58) — fresh products, dark bread, cheeses. Mon-Sat.

Maps: 📍 Bernardine Garden Vilnius

👶 Kids: 1. Līvu Akvaparks (Jūrmala, near Riga) - One of the largest water parks in Northern Europe, great for kids. 2. Riga Zoo (Mežaparks) - A large zoo with many animals and walking paths. 3. Esplanāde Park in Riga - Good for a short walk and has some play areas.

📋 Practical Info

🅿️ Accommodation: 1. Riga City Camping (Ķīpsala, Riga) - 📍 Maps Approx. €25-30/night. Features: electricity, water, WiFi, showers, close to city center. 2. Riverside Camping (Zunds canal, Riga) - 📍 Maps Approx. €30-35/night. Features: electricity, water, WiFi, camper service points.

⛽ Fuel: Main fuel station chains in Lithuania and Latvia include Circle K, Neste, Viada, and Orlen. There are no significant remote stretches without fuel on the main A2/A7 route between Vilnius and Riga. Approximate diesel price is €1.85 - €1.96 per liter.

🛣️ Tolls: For camper vans up to 3.5 tonnes, there are no vignette requirements or road tolls on motorways and expressways in Lithuania and Latvia. The route is generally toll-free for standard family camper vans.

⏰ Timing: Suggest departing Vilnius around 9:00 AM. The drive to Riga takes about 3.5 to 4 hours (approx. 300 km). Expected arrival in Riga around 1:00 PM - 2:00 PM, allowing time for a lunch stop. If visiting Rundāle Palace on the way, add 2-3 hours to the trip. Check museum closing times if planning afternoon visits in Riga.

🛒 Supermarkets: Main supermarket chains in Lithuania and Latvia include Maxima, Rimi, Iki (Lithuania), and Lidl. You will find large Maxima XXX or Rimi Hypermarkets on the outskirts of both Vilnius and Riga, which are easy to access with a camper van for stocking up.

🧺 Laundry: Self-service laundries are not very common along the highway. It is recommended to use the laundry facilities at your campsite (e.g., Riga City Camping usually has washing machines for a small fee) or look for a "Speed Queen" laundromat in Riga city center.

💧 Water/Dump: Most campgrounds like Riga City Camping and Riverside Camping offer dedicated water fill and grey/black water dump stations for guests. Dedicated service points outside campgrounds are rare, so it is best to use the facilities at your chosen campsite.

🏥 Safety: Nearest major hospital in Riga: Riga East Clinical University Hospital (Rīgas Austrumu klīniskā universitātes slimnīca), Hipokrāta iela 2, Riga. Emergency number in Latvia: 112 (General) or 113 (Ambulance). Warning: Watch out for wildlife (moose/deer) on rural roads, especially at dusk/dawn. Some road sections may be bumpy.

💰 Daily budget: €120-150

D4 · 30/06 · Vilnius → Riga 🇱🇹→🇱🇻

345 km · 4h 30m · Free

☀️ 22°C / 12°C · Good weather · 18h daylight

🏛️ ⭐ Hill of Crosses (Šiauliai) — 30 min stop, impressive 🏛️ ‍👩‍👧‍👦 Riga Motor Museum — amazing Soviet cars 🏛️ Art Nouveau district Alberta iela 🌭 Riga street food: Piragi (bacon rolls) from Central Market stalls ~€1-2 each. Lido (Krasta iela 76) — huge self-service ~€8/pax, playground for kids! Market: Rīgas Centrāltirgus (Nēģu iela 7, Zeppelin hangar!) — 5 pavilions: fish, meat, dairy, dark bread, vegetables. Mon-Sun. A must-see! 🛍️ Flea market: Latgale Tirgus (Firsa Sadovņikova iela 9) — legendary Baltic flea market! Soviet memorabilia, vinyl records, coins, vintage items. Tue-Sun 8:00-17:00 — 📍 Maps

🛴 Scooters: compact Riga center / Tallinn Pirita promenade → see rentals

Maps: 📍 Hill of Crosses Siauliai

👶 Kids: Children's Museum Miiamilla in Kadriorg Park offers creative activities and an awesome playground. For a rainy day, the Super Skypark indoor play centre in Tallinn is a great alternative.

📋 Practical Info

🅿️ Accommodation: Pirita Harbor Camping (Tallinn) - 📍 Maps Approx €35/night. Features: electricity, water, showers, located by the sea. Alternative: Tallinn City Camping - 📍 Maps Approx €29/night. Features: electricity, basic facilities, close to city center.

⛽ Fuel: Main fuel station chains in Estonia include Circle K, Neste, Alexela, and Jetoil. There are no remote stretches without fuel on the Via Baltica (E67) route. Diesel price is approximately €1.77 - €1.80 per liter.

🛣️ Tolls: Private cars and camper vans under 3.5t GVW drive all roads in Estonia and Latvia completely toll-free. There is no motorway vignette required for passenger vehicles or light campers. Cost: €0.

⏰ Timing: Depart Riga around 09:00. The drive takes about 4.5 hours (310 km) along the scenic coastal route (Via Baltica/E67). Arrive in Tallinn around 14:00-15:00, allowing time for a lunch stop and settling into the campsite before exploring the city.

🛒 Supermarkets: Main supermarket chains in Estonia are Coop, Maxima, Selver, Rimi, and Prisma. Rimi and Maxima are frequently found along the E67 route from Riga to Tallinn. Selver is available near Pirita Harbor Camping.

🧺 Laundry: Laundromat Magistral (Sõpruse pst 201, Tallinn) or Laundrix (Tartu mnt 24, Tallinn) offer self-service laundry facilities.

💧 Water/Dump: Pirita Harbor Camping offers fresh water fill and grey/black water dump facilities. Most major gas stations (like Circle K) along the route also have basic water services, but dedicated dumping is best done at the campsite.

🏥 Safety: Nearest hospital: Ida-Tallinna Keskhaigla (East Tallinn Central Hospital) Emergency Medicine Centre, Ravi 18, Tallinn. Emergency number: 112. Warnings: Watch out for wildlife (moose/deer) especially at dawn and dusk along the forested sections of the Via Baltica.

💰 Daily budget: €120-150

D5 · 01/07 · Riga → Tallinn 🇱🇻→🇪🇪

310 km · 4h 30m · Free

☀️ 21°C / 12°C · Good weather · 18h 30m daylight

🛣️ Via Baltica (E67) 🏛️ ‍👩‍👧‍👦 ⭐ Lennusadam (Seaplane Harbour) — submarine + seaplanes 🏛️ Old Town Tallinn (Unesco) 🌭 Tallinn street food: Kompressor (Rataskaevu 3) — giant savory/sweet pancakes ~€6-8, take-away! Street food at Balti Jaama Turg — international stalls ~€7-10. Kohuke (ricotta+chocolate bars, €0.50!) at Selver. Market: Balti Jaama Turg (Kopli 1) — street food + fresh products + crafts. Mon-Sun. 🛍️ Flea market: Balti Jaam Market (upper floor) — vintage clothing, Soviet memorabilia, antiques. Open daily — 📍 Maps. Also: Telliskivi kirbukas and Kalamaja Bazaar (vintage shops in the hipster district).

🛴 Scooters: Tallinn Pirita promenade and old town → see rentals

Maps: 📍 Seaplane Harbour Tallinn

👶 Kids: 1. Lappeenranta Sandcastle (Hiekkalinna): A massive sand sculpture exhibition built every summer near the harbor, featuring a new theme each year. Free entry and very popular with kids. 2. Myllysaari Family Park: Features a great playground, a public beach on Lake Saimaa, and walking paths.

📋 Practical Info

🅿️ Accommodation: Huhtiniemi Camping (Kuusimäenkatu 18, 53810 Lappeenranta). 📍 Maps Price: ~€35-40/night. Features: electricity, fresh water, grey/black water dump, WiFi, playground, saunas, and direct access to Lake Saimaa.

⛽ Fuel: Main fuel station chains in Finland include ABC, Neste, Teboil, Shell, and St1. There are plenty of stations along the highway from Helsinki to Lappeenranta; no remote stretches without fuel. Approximate diesel price: €2.28 - €2.35 per liter.

🛣️ Tolls: Finland has no road tolls or vignette requirements for passenger cars or camper vans. The route from Helsinki to Lappeenranta is completely toll-free. Cost: €0.

⏰ Timing: Suggest taking a morning ferry from Tallinn to Helsinki (e.g., 07:30 or 10:30 departure, 2-2.5 hours duration). Arrive in Helsinki by noon. Drive to Lappeenranta (225 km, ~2.5-3 hours). Arrive in Lappeenranta around 15:30-16:00 to visit the Sandcastle and harbor area before checking into the campsite.

🛒 Supermarkets: Main supermarket chains in Finland are Prisma, K-Citymarket, S-market, K-Supermarket, and Lidl. There is a large Prisma hypermarket in Lappeenranta (Puhakankatu 9) which is excellent for stocking up on supplies.

🧺 Laundry: Washing machines and dryers are available for guest use at Huhtiniemi Camping (tokens usually purchased at reception).

💧 Water/Dump: Fresh water fill and grey/black water dump facilities are available at Huhtiniemi Camping. Public service points are rare, so it is best to use the campsite facilities.

🏥 Safety: Nearest hospital: South Karelia Central Hospital (Etelä-Karjalan keskussairaala), Valto Käkelän katu 1, 53130 Lappeenranta. Emergency number in Finland: 112. Warnings: Watch out for moose and elk on the roads, especially at dawn and dusk. Speed cameras are very common on Finnish highways.

💰 Daily budget: €260-310

D6 · 02/07 · Tallinn → Lappeenranta 🇪🇪→🇫🇮

250 km · 3h + ferry 2h · Ferry Tallinn–Helsinki ~€100-150 (van+4)

☀️ 20°C / 12°C · Variable · 19h daylight

🥾 Trekking: Punkaharju Ridge — glacial esker, 7 km flat, perfect with kids → trail details

⛴️ Ferry Tallinn → Helsinki (Tallink/Viking Line, 2h) 🍽️ Helsinki stop: Market Square + Cathedral 🚗 Helsinki → Lappeenranta (230 km, 2h 30m) 🌭 Helsinki street food: Stalls at Kauppatori harbor — lohikeitto (salmon soup) ~€8, grilled salmon ~€10. Karjalanpiirakka (Karelian pies with egg butter) ~€3 from stalls. Market: Vanha Kauppahalli (Old Market Hall, Eteläranta 1) — smoked salmon, reindeer, cheeses. Mon-Sat 8-18. 🛍️ Flea market: Hietalahti Flea Market (Lönnrotinkatu 34) — Helsinki's biggest outdoor flea market! Vintage, clothes, vinyl, curiosities. Daily May-Sep — 📍 Maps 🎢 Amusement park: Linnanmäki — Finland's oldest and most popular amusement park! 40+ rides. FREE entry (€5 area), ride wristband ~€42/pax. Open 13:00-20:00+ in summer — 📍 Maps

Ferry: Book at tallink.com or vikingline.com. Van + 4 pax ~€100-150 in summer (book in advance!).

Maps: 📍 Market Square Helsinki

👶 Kids: 1. Kesämaa Water and Amusement Park in Punkaharju: Features heated pools, water slides, and climbing areas perfect for kids. 2. Lusto Finnish Forest Museum: Very close to the campsites, offering interactive and educational exhibits about forestry that are engaging for children.

📋 Practical Info

🅿️ Accommodation: 1. Punkaharju Resort (Tuunaansaarentie 4, 58390 Punkaharju). 📍 Maps Price: ~€45-55/night. Features: electricity, water, WiFi, playground, saunas, lakeside pitches. 2. Holiday Resort Harjun Portti (Tuunaansaarentie 2, 58390 Punkaharju). 📍 Maps Price: ~€40-50/night. Features: electricity, water, restaurant, equipment rental.

⛽ Fuel: Main fuel station chains in Finland include ABC, Neste, St1, and Teboil. There are no remote stretches without fuel on this short route. Approximate diesel price: €2.28 - €2.35 per liter.

🛣️ Tolls: Finland does not have a toll road system or vignette requirement for passenger vehicles or camper vans. The route is completely free of charge. Cost: €0.

⏰ Timing: Suggested departure from Lappeenranta at 10:00 AM. The drive is short (approx. 90 km, 1.5 hours). Expected arrival in Punkaharju around 11:30 AM. Time-sensitive: Check Lusto Forest Museum hours (typically open until 17:00 or 18:00 in summer) and Kesämaa water park opening hours.

🛒 Supermarkets: Main supermarket chains in Finland are S-market, K-Supermarket, Prisma, and Lidl. It is recommended to do a larger grocery run at Prisma or K-Citymarket in Lappeenranta before departing. There is also an S-market and K-Market in Punkaharju town center for daily needs.

🧺 Laundry: Self-service laundry facilities (washing machines and dryers) are available at Punkaharju Resort and Harjun Portti campsites for a small additional fee (approx. €5 per load).

💧 Water/Dump: Fresh water fill and grey/black water dump facilities are available at the recommended campsites (Punkaharju Resort and Harjun Portti). Additionally, some larger ABC service stations along the route may offer basic water services.

🏥 Safety: Nearest hospital with an emergency room is Savonlinna Central Hospital (approx. 35 km from Punkaharju). The national emergency number is 112. Warnings: Be highly vigilant for moose and deer crossing the roads, especially during dawn and dusk. The roads in the Lake District can be winding.

💰 Daily budget: €150-180

D7 · 03/07 · Lappeenranta → Punkaharju 🇫🇮

100 km · 1h 30m · Free

👶 Kids: 1. Visit the Olavinlinna Castle in Savonlinna, which is exciting for kids to explore. 2. Enjoy a relaxing day at the campsite beach (e.g., Lake Saimaa) with swimming and playground activities. 3. Try a short family-friendly nature walk in the surrounding pine forests.

📋 Practical Info

🅿️ Accommodation: 1. Huhtiniemi Camping (Lappeenranta): GPS 61.0556, 28.1569. Approx. €35-45/night. Features: electricity, water, WiFi, playground, located by Lake Saimaa. 2. Savonlinna Camping Vuohimäki: GPS 61.8519, 28.8258. Approx. €30-40/night. Features: electricity, water, lakeside pitches, playground.

⛽ Fuel: Main fuel station chains in Finland include ABC, Neste, Shell, and Teboil. Remote stretches without fuel are rare in the southern Saimaa region, but it's good practice to keep the tank half full. Approximate diesel price: €2.30 - €2.65 per liter (varies by station and exact date).

🛣️ Tolls: Road use in Finland is free of charge for all vehicles, including camper vans. There are no toll roads or vignette requirements. Approximate cost: €0.

⏰ Timing: As this is a rest day, there is no strict schedule. Suggested departure from the previous stop: 10:00 AM. Expected arrival at the campsite: 12:00 PM. If visiting Olavinlinna Castle in Savonlinna, check opening hours (typically 10:00 AM - 6:00 PM in summer).

🛒 Supermarkets: Main supermarket chains in Finland are S-Market, Prisma (S Group), K-Citymarket, K-Supermarket (K Group), and Lidl. You can find large Prisma and K-Citymarket stores in both Lappeenranta and Savonlinna for stocking up on supplies.

🧺 Laundry: 24 Pesula is a popular self-service laundromat chain in Finland. There is a location in Lappeenranta at Prisma Lappeenranta (Puhakankatu 9). A standard wash takes about 30 minutes and costs around €6-8.

💧 Water/Dump: Most campsites in the Saimaa region, such as Huhtiniemi Camping and Vuohimäki Camping, offer dedicated water fill and grey/black water dump stations for guests. Public dump stations are rare in Finland, so it is recommended to use campsite facilities.

🏥 Safety: Nearest hospitals: South Karelia Central Hospital in Lappeenranta or Savonlinna Central Hospital. Emergency number for Finland is 112. Warnings: Watch out for wildlife (moose and deer) on the roads, especially at dusk and dawn. Roads are generally in good condition but can be narrow in rural areas.

💰 Daily budget: €130-160

D8 · 04/07 · Lake District (Saimaa) 🇫🇮

0 km · Stationary day

Spots: any pier or shore of Saimaa. ♨️ Finnish sauna on the lake + dip → see ♨️ details 🌲 ‍👩‍👧‍👦 Canoe/kayak rental at local facilities 🍳 Lohikeitto (creamy salmon soup) — easy to make in the van with fresh salmon from S-Market! Tip: Fishing with mato-onki (simple rod with float and worm) is FREE for everyone in Finland, no license needed. Perfect for kids!

🛶 Kayak/canoe rental: Saimaa, calm lake perfect for families (~€40-60/day) → see rentals

Maps: 📍 Saimaa Lake Finland

👶 Kids: Nallikari Beach is a famous kilometres-long sandy beach right next to the campsite. Other kid-friendly activities in Oulu include Ainolan Puisto and Hupisaaret Park.

📋 Practical Info

🛣️ Tolls: No tolls. Finland does not charge road tolls on any publicly operated motorway, highway, or state road. Cost: €0.

⏰ Timing: Suggest departing Laghi early morning (e.g., 8:00 AM) for the 450km drive. Expected arrival in Oulu around 2:00 PM - 3:00 PM. Reception at Nallikari is open 8 AM to 11 PM in summer.

🛒 Supermarkets: Main chains: K-Supermarket, S-market. Nearest to campsite: K-Supermarket Toppila (Satamatie 26, 90520 Oulu, ~1.5km away). S-market Tuira is open 24/7.

🧺 Laundry: Nallikari Holiday Village has a laundry room in the service building available for a small fee. Alternatively, 24 Pesula operates self-service laundromats in Oulu.

💧 Water/Dump: Nallikari Holiday Village offers disposal points for chemical toilet and greywater waste, and a freshwater supply point.

🏥 Safety: Nearest hospital: Oulu University Hospital (OYS). Emergency number: 112. Warnings: Watch for wildlife (reindeer in the north), headlights must always be on.

💰 Daily budget: €120-150

D9 · 05/07 · Lakes → Oulu 🇫🇮

450 km · 5h 30m · Free

☀️ 20°C / 10°C · Short rain · 21h daylight

🛣️ Drive through boreal forests 🏛️ Possible stop at Jyväskylä (Alvar Aalto Museum) 🌭 Oulu stop: try grillimakkara (giant sausage) in a picnic area with public grill

Maps: 📍 Oulu

👶 Kids: 1. Ranua Wildlife Park (Zoo): The main attraction, featuring Arctic animals like polar bears, lynx, and wolverines. A family ticket (2 adults, up to 8 kids aged 4-14) costs €74-€80. Kids under 4 are free.
2. Playground: Ranua Resort Camping has an on-site children's playground.

📋 Practical Info

🅿️ Accommodation: Ranua Resort - Camping Wildlife Park
📍 Maps (N65°56'40.19", E26°27'41.72")
Price: Caravan pitch with electricity €30/night + €5/person fee (approx. €50 for a family of 4).
Features: Electricity, kitchen, dining area, grill, saunas, showers, laundry, playground, WiFi, and waste disposal. Located right next to the wildlife park.

⛽ Fuel: Main fuel station chains in Finland include ABC, Neste, Teboil, and Shell. The route from Oulu to Ranua (approx. 160 km) has regular stations, but it's advisable to fill up in Oulu or Pudasjärvi before heading into more remote Lapland areas. Diesel price in Finland is approximately €1.50 - €1.60 per liter (2024-2025 estimates).

🛣️ Tolls: Finland does not have toll roads for passenger cars or camper vans. The route from Oulu to Ranua is toll-free.

⏰ Timing: Depart Oulu around 9:00 AM. The drive to Ranua is about 160 km and takes roughly 2 hours. Arrive at Ranua Resort around 11:00 AM. Spend the afternoon at the Ranua Wildlife Park (Zoo). Check zoo opening hours locally as they may vary by season.

🛒 Supermarkets: Main supermarket chains in Finland are S-Market and K-Market (K-Supermarket/K-Citymarket). In Ranua, you will find both an S-Market and a K-Market for grocery shopping. In Oulu, there are larger hypermarkets like Prisma and K-Citymarket for stocking up before the drive.

🧺 Laundry: Ranua Resort Camping Wildlife Park has on-site laundry facilities (washing machine available for ~€3).

💧 Water/Dump: Ranua Resort Camping Wildlife Park provides dedicated facilities for campers, including fresh water fill points and a toilet disposal station (black/grey water dump).

🏥 Safety: Emergency number in Finland is 112. The nearest major hospital with full emergency services is Oulu University Hospital (OYS) in Oulu. For non-life-threatening urgent care, contact the local health center in Ranua or call the Medical Helpline 116 117. Warning: Watch out for reindeer and moose on the roads, especially in Lapland.

💰 Daily budget: €170-200 (Campsite: ~€40-45, Fuel: ~€25, Food/Supermarket: ~€40-50, Activities/Zoo Family Ticket: €74-80)

💧 Water/Dump: Ounaskoski Camping offers fresh water and grey/black water disposal (included if staying, or for a small fee if just passing through). BestPark Arctic Circle also provides water and dumping facilities.

🏥 Safety: Nearest hospital: Lapland Central Hospital (Ounasrinteentie 22, 96400 Rovaniemi), which has a 24/7 emergency room. Emergency number in Finland is 112. Watch out for reindeer on the roads, as they roam freely in Lapland.

D12 · 08/07 · Rovaniemi 🇫🇮

0 km · Stationary day

🌲 ‍👩‍👧‍👦 ⭐ 📍 Santa Claus Village — post office, reindeer, Arctic Circle line 🏛️ ⭐ Arktikum — Arctic museum/science centre (€22 adult, €10 child — ⚠️ closed Monday) 🎣 Fishing: Kemijoki river in Rovaniemi (salmon running in July!). Local permit needed in addition to state fee — ask tourist office.

Maps: 📍 Santa Claus Main Office

⛽ Fuel: Main fuel station chains in Finland include ABC, Neste, Teboil, and St1. Fuel stations are available in Rovaniemi, Sodankylä, Saariselkä, Ivalo, and Inari. There are no extremely remote stretches without fuel on the E75, but it's good practice to fill up in Sodankylä or Ivalo. Approximate diesel price: €2.30 - €2.65 per liter (2024 data).

🛣️ Tolls: Finland does not have toll roads or vignette requirements for passenger cars or camper vans. The roads are free to use. Cost: €0.

🛒 Supermarkets: Main supermarket chains in Finland are K-Market, S-Market, and Prisma. Along the route: K-Citymarket/Prisma in Rovaniemi (good for stocking up), S-Market in Sodankylä, K-Supermarket in Ivalo, and K-Market in Inari (near the campsites).

🧺 Laundry: Self-service laundries are not common along the route. It is recommended to use the laundry facilities at the campsites (e.g., Holiday Village Inari or Uruniemi Camping). Verify availability locally.

💧 Water/Dump: Water fill and dump points are available at Uruniemi Camping and Holiday Village Inari. Most campgrounds in Finland offer these services for guests. Dedicated public dump stations are rare, so it is best to use campsite facilities.

🏥 Safety: Nearest hospital/health center is in Ivalo (Ivalon terveyskeskus), about 40 km south of Inari. The general emergency number in Finland is 112. Warnings: Watch out for reindeer on the roads (very common in Lapland), and be prepared for changing weather conditions even in summer.

D13 · 09/07 · Rovaniemi → Inari 🇫🇮

330 km · 4h 30m · Free

🏛️ Siida Museum (Sámi culture + arctic nature) ⚠️ Reindeer on the road (drive carefully!) 🎣 Fishing: Lake Inari — one of Finland’s best lakes for lake trout and Arctic char. State fee + local Inari permit (buy at eraluvat.fi, ~€10/day). ⚠️ Mosquitoes: from here until G15, DEET 30%+ and mosquito nets mandatory.

Tundrea Holiday Resort (approx. 69.0450, 20.8000) - ~€40/night, features electric hookups, chemical toilet emptying, restaurant, saunas.

⛽ Fuel: Main chains in Finland include Neste, ABC, and Teboil. Approximate diesel price in Finland is €2.30 - €2.65 per liter (2024-2025 data).

🛣️ Tolls: Free (No toll roads in Finland for campervans).

⏰ Timing: Suggest departing Inari around 9:00 AM. The drive is about 428 km and takes roughly 5.5 to 6 hours of pure driving. 🛒 Supermarkets: K-Market Kilpishalli (Käsivarrentie 14205, Kilpisjärvi) is the main supermarket in the village, offering a good selection of fresh food, meat, and an Alko shop. Open daily.

🧺 Laundry: N/A (No dedicated public self-service laundry found in Kilpisjärvi; verify locally at campsites like Tundrea or Retkeilykeskus if they offer guest laundry facilities).

🏥 Safety: Emergency number in Finland is 112. For non-urgent medical advice, call 116117. Note that for Kilpisjärvi, the nearest major hospital is often across the border in Tromsø, Norway, rather than in Finland due to the remote location. Watch out for reindeer on the roads and changing weather conditions.

D14 · 10/07 · Inari → Kilpisjärvi 🇫🇮

300 km · 4h · Free

☀️ 18°C / 8°C · Variable · 24h daylight · ⚠️ Mosquitoes

🌲 Treriksröset — point where Finland, Sweden and Norway meet (3 km easy trek) 🎣 Fishing: Lake Kilpisjärvi — Arctic char. Local permit ~€8/day available at visitor center.

Maps: 📍 Kilpisjärvi

👶 Kids: Polaria (Arctic aquarium with bearded seals) is highly recommended for kids. Fjellheisen cable car is another great activity offering panoramic views of the city and fjords.

📋 Practical Info

🅿️ Accommodation: Tromsø Lodge & Camping 📍 Maps. Approx €35-45/night. Features: electricity, water, WiFi, playground, sanitary facilities.

⛽ Fuel: Main chains in Norway: Circle K, Shell, Esso, YX. Tip: Refuel in Kilpisjärvi (Finland) before crossing the border as diesel is often cheaper. Diesel in Norway is approx €1.90 - €2.15/liter. No major remote stretches without fuel on this specific route.

🛣️ Tolls: Norway uses the AutoPASS system (automatic camera tolling). Tromsø has a toll ring (Bypakke Tromsø). Approximate cost for a camper van for this route/city entry is €5-10.

⏰ Timing: Suggest departing Kilpisjärvi at 09:00. The drive is about 2.5-3 hours (163 km). Expected arrival in Tromsø around 12:00. Time-sensitive: Polaria aquarium feeding times (usually 12:30 and 15:30).

🛒 Supermarkets: Main chains in Norway: REMA 1000, Kiwi, Extra. Suggest shopping at K-Market in Kilpisjärvi before crossing, or at Eurospar/REMA 1000 upon arrival in Tromsø.

🧺 Laundry: Tromsø Lodge & Camping offers self-service laundry facilities (washing machines and dryers) for guests.

💧 Water/Dump: Fresh water fill and grey/black water dump available at Tromsø Lodge & Camping.

🏥 Safety: Nearest hospital: University Hospital of North Norway (UNN) in Tromsø. Emergency numbers in Norway: 113 (Medical), 112 (Police), 110 (Fire). Medical advice: 116 117. Warnings: Watch out for reindeer on the roads near the border.

D15 · 11/07 · Kilpisjärvi → Tromsø 🇫🇮→🇳🇴

160 km · 2h 30m · AutoPASS (register at autopass.no)

☀️ 15°C / 9°C · Wind, possible rain · 24h daylight ☀️ (midnight sun)

🥾 Trekking: ⭐ Sherpatrappa 600m elevation, Tromsø view (solo, 2h, start 5:00) · Fjellheisen cable car + high altitude trails (family, 30 min) · Prestvannet lake loop 3 km (family) → trail details

🏛️ Arctic Cathedral (Ishavskatedralen) 🛣️ Fjellheisen cable car — panoramic view 🏛️ ‍👩‍👧‍👦 ⭐ Polaria (arctic aquarium, bearded seals) — 395 NOK adult (~€34), 220 NOK child 3-15 (~€19). Family ticket 925 NOK (~€80) ➕ alt: Polar Museum ➕ alt: Sommarøy (white beaches, 1h) ♨️ Pust Tromsø — floating sauna on the fjord → see ♨️ details 🎣 Fishing: from the Tromsø pier or shore — cod, pollack. FREE at sea, no license required in Norway! 🌭 Tromsø street food: Raketten Pølsebod (hot dog stand, downtown) — pølse ~NOK 60-80 (~€5.6-€7.4). Fish & chips take-away at the harbor ~NOK 150. Rein-burger (reindeer hamburger) from food trucks ~NOK 130. Market/supermarket: Rema 1000 or Kiwi (the cheapest) — brunost, smoked salmon, fresh bread. Tip: in Norway cooking in the van is almost mandatory!

Tolls: From here on AutoPASS — automatic toll (cameras). Register at autopass.no for 20% discount. Without registration: invoice sent home, full price.

Maps: 📍 Fjellheisen Tromsø

👶 Kids: 1. Senja Husky Adventure: Family-run dog sled kennel offering visits and activities with huskies. 2. Ersfjordstranda: A beautiful beach with golden sand, perfect for kids to play (even if the water is cold), featuring a unique gold-plated toilet facility.

📋 Practical Info

🅿️ Accommodation: 1. Fjordbotn Camping: Located near Botnhamn (approx. 69.4914, 17.8967), ~€30-40/night, offers electricity, water, WiFi, and a playground. 2. Skaland Camping: Located in Skaland (approx. 69.4444, 17.2981), ~€30-40/night, features indoor bathrooms, kitchen, and electric hookups.

⛽ Fuel: Main fuel chains include Circle K, Shell, and Bunker Oil. Diesel price is approximately 22-23 NOK per liter (~€1.90-€2.00). It is highly recommended to fill up in Tromsø or Finnsnes before exploring the more remote western coast of Senja, as fuel stations are sparse on the scenic route.

🛣️ Tolls: Norway uses the AutoPASS system for tolls and ferries. The Brensholmen-Botnhamn ferry fare is collected automatically via AutoPASS/license plate reading. Approximate cost for a camper van on the ferry is around 200-400 NOK (€17-€35) depending on length and AutoPASS discount. Road tolls are minimal on Senja itself.

⏰ Timing: Depart Tromsø around 08:00 or 09:00 to catch the morning ferry from Brensholmen to Botnhamn (e.g., 09:45 departure, 45-minute crossing). Arrive in Senja by mid-morning to maximize the day exploring the scenic route. Note that the ferry can be crowded in summer, so arrive early.

🛒 Supermarkets: Main supermarket chains include Rema 1000, Extra, and Eurospar (cheaper options are Rema 1000 and Extra). Stock up in Tromsø or Finnsnes before heading to western Senja. On Senja, there are smaller local shops like Joker in Skaland, Husøy, and Gibostad, but they have limited selection and higher prices.

🧺 Laundry: Clean Kokos in Tromsø (Grønnegata 3B) is a modern self-service laundromat open 6 AM to 10 PM. On Senja, self-service laundry is scarce; it is best to use the laundry facilities at established campsites like Fjordbotn Camping or Skaland Camping.

💧 Water/Dump: Many campsites like Fjordbotn Camping or Skaland Camping offer fresh water fill and grey/black water dump stations. Additionally, some public rest areas along the Norwegian Scenic Route on Senja (e.g., Ersfjordstranda) have service facilities, though dedicated dump stations are best found at established campsites or larger gas stations.

🏥 Safety: The nearest major hospital is the University Hospital of North Norway (UNN) in Tromsø (approx. 2-3 hours drive or ferry back). For minor emergencies, there is a local medical center (legevakt) in Finnsnes. Emergency number in Norway is 113 (medical), 112 (police), 110 (fire). Warning: Roads on Senja's west coast are very narrow and winding; drive carefully with a camper van.

💰 Daily budget: €130-180

D16 · 12/07 · Tromsø → Senja 🇳🇴

170 km · 3h · AutoPASS + short ferry

☀️ 14°C / 9°C · Variable, windy · 24h daylight

🛣️ ⭐ Senja National Tourist Route (one of the 18 Nasjonale Turistveger) 🛣️ ⭐ Tungeneset — panoramic platform on the Devil's Teeth (Okshornan) 🌲 ⭐ Ersfjordstranda — spectacular Arctic white beach 🌲 Segla — trek (5h round trip, challenging, only fit adults) 🌲 "Norway in miniature": fjords, mountains, beaches all on one island 🎣 ⭐ Fishing: Senja is EXCEPTIONAL for shore fishing. Arctic cod, pollack, mackerel from village piers (Husøy, Mefjordvær). FREE, no license. 🛒 Senja: buy fresh salmon at Rema 1000/Kiwi (~NOK 150 (~€14)/kg) and grill in picnic area Tip: Senja is less touristy than the Lofoten but equally spectacular. In July you will have the midnight sun — you can fish at 11:00 PM with full light!

🛶 Kayak rental: Hamn i Senja, midnight sun kayaking (~NOK 500-800) → see rentals

Maps: 📍 Tungeneset Senja

👶 Kids: 1. Whale Safari (Whale watching) from Andenes harbor - a thrilling experience for kids to see whales in their natural habitat. 2. Relaxing and playing on the beautiful white sandy beach right next to Andenes Camping. 3. Puffin watching tours are also available and very popular with families.

📋 Practical Info

🅿️ Accommodation: Andenes Camping. 📍 Maps Price: ~300-450 NOK (€25-40) per night. Features: Located on a stunning white sandy beach, electricity, water filling, dump station, WiFi, toilets/showers, washing machine, and a lounge room with ocean views. Grocery store 200m away.

⛽ Fuel: Main fuel chains in Norway include Circle K, Shell, Esso, and Uno-X. Diesel price is approximately 19.88 NOK per liter (~€1.70 - €1.80). Fuel stations are generally available in larger towns like Andenes, but it's wise to fill up before long remote stretches on Senja.

🛣️ Tolls: The main toll cost for this day is the Gryllefjord - Andenes ferry. For a camper van between 6.01 - 8m, the full price is 1985 NOK (~€170). With an AutoPASS agreement, you get a 50% discount (992.50 NOK / ~€85). Road tolls in Norway use the AutoPASS system (automatic camera tolling).

⏰ Timing: The Gryllefjord to Andenes ferry is very popular and small, with no pre-booking possible. In peak summer (June 13 - Aug 17), there are typically 3 departures. A common morning departure is at 08:45 (arriving 10:25) or 11:00, and an afternoon one at 17:00 (arriving 18:40). It is highly recommended to arrive at Gryllefjord 2-3 hours early, as many campervans queue overnight.

🛒 Supermarkets: In Andenes, you will find major Norwegian supermarket chains such as REMA 1000 and Coop Extra. There is a well-stocked grocery store just 200 meters away from Andenes Camping.

🧺 Laundry: Andenes Camping has a washroom with a washing machine available for guests. For public laundromats, they are rare in Norway, so utilizing the campsite facilities is highly recommended.

💧 Water/Dump: Andenes Camping offers a dump station for motorhomes and caravans, as well as fresh water filling. There is also a public dump station in Andenes (near 38 Sekundær Fylkesveg 82) where water supply and waste disposal are available for a fee via PayPal.

🏥 Safety: The nearest local medical center (Legevakt) is in Andenes. For serious emergencies, the nearest major hospital is in Stokmarknes (Vesterålen Hospital). Emergency numbers in Norway: 113 (Medical/Ambulance), 112 (Police), 110 (Fire). Warning: Narrow roads on Senja and potential wildlife (reindeer/moose) on the roads.

💰 Daily budget: €180-230 (Campsite: ~€30-40, Ferry Gryllefjord-Andenes for camper >6m: ~€170-220 depending on exact length and AutoPASS discount, Food/Fuel: ~€30-50). Note: Whale watching tours would add significantly to the budget if chosen.

D17 · 13/07 · Senja → Andenes 🇳🇴

⛴️ Ferry Gryllefjord → Andenes (1h 40m). NOK 1985 for van 6-8m (~€180), passengers included. 🛣️ Andøya National Tourist Route — west coast of Andøya, Arctic white beaches, fishing villages, marshes. One of the 18 Nasjonale Turistveger. 🚗 Entering Vesterålen 🎣 Fishing: Andenes pier in the evening — cod, coalfish. FREE.

Ferry: Gryllefjord–Andenes on torghatten.no. ⚠️ NOT bookable (first come, first served). In high season arrive 3-4h before departure to secure a spot. Small ferry, often full in July!

Maps: 📍 Andenes Lighthouse

👶 Kids: 1. Spaceship Aurora (Andøya Space Visitor Center): Interactive astronaut training, films, and space exhibits suitable for kids. 2. Whale Safari: Whale2Sea or Arctic Whale Tours offer family-friendly boat trips to see sperm whales (infants 0-2 free, discounts for kids/youth).

📋 Practical Info

🅿️ Accommodation: Andenes Camping (Bleiksveien 32, 8480 Andenes). 📍 Maps Price: ~400 NOK (€35) per night for campervan including 2 persons and electricity. Features: Electricity, water, WiFi, toilets, showers, playground, washing machine, greywater/chemical disposal, located on a white sandy beach.

⛽ Fuel: Main chains include Circle K, Shell, and Esso. Diesel price is approximately 19.88 NOK/liter (~€1.70-1.80/liter). Fuel stations are available in Andenes, but fill up before long remote stretches in Northern Norway.

🛣️ Tolls: AutoPASS system applies in Norway. Motorhomes under 3.5t or registered with an AutoPASS tag pay the same rates as regular cars. Ensure your camper is registered with a toll chip provider (like AutoPASS or Epass24) to avoid higher fees and get discounts. Tolls for local driving around Andenes are minimal, but expect ~€5-10 if traveling from further away.

⏰ Timing: Morning (09:00-10:00): Depart for Whale Safari (tours usually last 3-5 hours, check specific departure time with operator). Afternoon (14:00-15:00): Visit Spaceship Aurora. Evening: Relax at the campsite or explore the white sandy beach at Andenes Camping.

🛒 Supermarkets: Coop Prix (Storgata 69, Andenes) and Bunnpris Andenes (Myrveien 1, Andenes) are the main supermarkets in town, conveniently located near the campsite and harbor.

🧺 Laundry: Andenes Camping has washing machines and tumble dryers available for guests. Public self-service laundromats are rare in Norway, so utilize the campsite facilities.

💧 Water/Dump: Andenes Camping offers grey water disposal, chemical toilet discharge, and fresh water supply. There is also a dump station at the local Coop grocery store in Andenes.

🏥 Safety: Emergency numbers: 113 (Medical), 112 (Police), 110 (Fire). Nearest local medical help is the Legevakt (out-of-hours medical service, call 116 117). For major emergencies, the nearest large hospitals are in Stokmarknes (Nordland Hospital Vesterålen) or Tromsø. Warning: Weather can change rapidly, dress warmly even in summer for the whale safari. Watch for wildlife (reindeer/moose) on roads.

💰 Daily budget: €180-250 (Campsite: ~€35-40, Fuel: ~€30, Food/Supermarket: ~€40-50, Whale Safari for family of 4: ~€100-150 depending on kids' ages and specific tour). Whale safari is a major expense but a highlight.

🛣️ Tolls: Norway uses the AutoPASS system for tolls. Register your campervan for an AutoPASS tag to get the regular car rate (and a 10% discount on ferries). 🛒 Supermarkets: Main supermarket chains are REMA 1000, Kiwi, and Extra. They are competitively priced and frequently found in larger towns. In Svolvær, you will find Kiwi and REMA 1000 within walking distance of the center.

🧺 Laundry: Self-service laundry is available at the tourist information center in Svolvær (purchase tokens before 6 PM, facility open 24/7, approx. 60 NOK per wash). Lyngvær Lofoten Bobilcamp also has laundry facilities.

💧 Water/Dump: Fresh water and grey/black water dumping are available at Lyngvær Lofoten Bobilcamp (included in price) and Svolvær Bobilpark. Public rest stops and gas stations in Norway also often have water facilities. Use the Park4Night app to locate specific public dump stations.

🏥 Safety: The nearest emergency clinic (legevakt) is in Gravdal at Risfaret 8, or call 116 117 for local out-of-hours medical service. In a life-threatening emergency, call 113. Be cautious of narrow roads, tunnels, and sudden weather changes in Lofoten.

D19 · 15/07 · Andenes → Svolvær (Lofoten) 🇳🇴

Tip: cooking in the van = the only sensible option (restaurants NOK 400-600/person!).

🛒 Supermarkets: In Svolvær, you can find large supermarkets like REMA 1000, Coop Extra, and Kiwi. In Henningsvær, there is a smaller Joker supermarket and local grocery stores like Leif Johansen & Co. Stock up in Svolvær for better prices and selection.

🧺 Laundry: In Svolvær's marina area, by the main square, there is a harbour service building equipped with two washing machines and two dryers open to travellers 24/7 (coins needed from the tourist centre before 6pm). Lyngvær Lofoten Bobilcamping also has laundry facilities.

🧺 Laundry: Self-service laundry is available at most major campsites in Lofoten (e.g., Moskenes Camping). In Svolvær, there is a Clean Kokos self-service laundromat, but near Nusfjord, rely on campsite facilities.

💧 Water/Dump: Most campsites in Lofoten, such as Moskenes Camping or Ramberg Gjestegård, offer water fill and dump stations for guests. Public dump stations can also be found at some larger gas stations or dedicated rest areas in the region. Verify locally for specific public points near Nusfjord.

🏥 Safety: The nearest hospital with an emergency room is in Gravdal (Nordlandssykehuset Lofoten, Risfaret 8, Gravdal). The medical emergency number in Norway is 113, and for urgent but non-life-threatening medical help, call 116 117. Warnings: Narrow roads, single-lane bridges, and unpredictable weather.

💰 Daily budget: €120-150

Note: Most supermarkets in Norway are closed on Sundays.

🧺 Laundry: Hotel Union in Geiranger offers a laundry service that is relatively cheap and has good dryers. Some campsites like Geiranger Camping or Vinje Camping may also have laundry facilities on-site. Alternatively, check for self-service laundromats in larger towns before arriving in Geiranger.

💧 Water/Dump: Many campgrounds in Geiranger (like Geiranger Camping) offer fresh water fill and grey/black water dump for guests. Public dump stations can be found using apps like park4night, and some rest stops along the E6/E136/Fv63 routes indicate disposal points. Note that water at some public dump stations may be turned off during colder months, but should be fully operational in summer.

🏥 Safety: Nearest major hospital is Ålesund Sjukehus (Ålesund Hospital) or Molde Hospital. In Geiranger, there is a local medical center/doctor. Emergency numbers in Norway: 113 (Ambulance/Medical), 112 (Police), 110 (Fire). For non-life-threatening medical help (Legevakt), call 116 117. Warnings: The Trollstigen pass has very narrow hairpin bends and steep inclines; drive carefully with a campervan. Weather can change rapidly.

Bag of fresh shrimp at Fisketorget ~NOK 100 (~€9.3) — eat them on Bryggen pier! Fiskekaker (fish cakes) take-away ~NOK 60 (~€5.6). Market: Fisketorget (Fish Market, Strandkaien 3) — shrimp, crab, salmon. Every day. Tip: Bergen with sun is a rare gift. If you have it, drop everything and go up Fløyen.

🛶🏄 Rentals: bikes, kayak (Ado Arena ~NOK 300/h) and SUP (Solheimsviken ~NOK 250/h) available → see rentals 🛴 Scooters: Bryggen and waterfront (flat center, avoid hills) → see rentals

Maps: 📍 Fløibanen

👶 Kids: Walk around Mosvatnet lake right next to the campsite, or visit the Norwegian Petroleum Museum in Stavanger which has great interactive exhibits for kids.

📋 Practical Info

🅿️ Accommodation: Mosvangen Camping Stavanger 📍 Maps. Price: ~€38 (450 NOK) per night. Features: electricity, water, WiFi, kitchen, toilets, showers, located by Mosvatnet lake.

⛽ Fuel: Main chains: Circle K, Shell, Esso, YX. No remote stretches without fuel on this route. Diesel price: ~€1.85/liter.

🛣️ Tolls: AutoPASS system applies for both road tolls and ferries (FerryPay/AutoPASS for ferry). The E39 route includes two ferries (Halhjem-Sandvikvåg and Arsvågen-Mortavika). Approximate total cost for camper van (tolls + ferries): ~€100-130.

⏰ Timing: Suggest departure from Bergen at 09:00. The drive takes about 5-6 hours including two ferry crossings. Expected arrival in Stavanger around 14:30. Ferries run frequently (every 20-30 mins) but expect summer queues.

🛒 Supermarkets: Main chains: REMA 1000, Kiwi, Coop Extra. Several options available along the E39 route and near the campsite in Stavanger.

🧺 Laundry: Laundry facilities are available directly at Mosvangen Camping.

💧 Water/Dump: Fresh water fill and grey/black water dump available at Mosvangen Camping.

🏥 Safety: Nearest hospital: Stavanger University Hospital (Stavanger universitetssjukehus). Emergency numbers: 112 (Police), 113 (Medical), 110 (Fire). Warnings: Watch for speed cameras and expect potential queues at ferry terminals.

💰 Daily budget: €250-280

D32 · 28/07 · Stavanger → Kristiansand 🇳🇴

☀️ 18°C / 12°C · 50% Cloudy · 18h 30m daylight

🥾 ⭐ Preikestolen (Pulpit Rock) — 4h round trip trek, 350m elevation, doable with motivated kids (6+). No railing at the top: hold little ones’ hands!

➕ alt: Petroleum Museum (Stavanger, if it rains)

Note: Preikestolen requires an early start (7:00) to avoid crowds. If children can't manage, the Petroleum Museum is a great interactive alternative.

Maps: 📍 Preikestolen Trailhead

👶 Kids: 1. **Tivoli Gardens:** A world-famous amusement park in the heart of Copenhagen, perfect for kids of all ages. 2. **National Museum of Denmark:** Features an excellent Children's Museum where kids can play in a Viking ship and explore interactive exhibits.

📋 Practical Info

🅿️ Accommodation: 1. **DCU-Camping Absalon (Copenhagen):** Korsdalsvej 132, 2610 Rødovre. 📍 Maps Price: ~€45-60/night. Features: Electricity, water, WiFi, modern facilities, playground, close to public transport into the city. 2. **Camperparking.dk Copenhagen:** Bådehavnsgade 55, 2450 København. 📍 Maps Price: ~€39/night (290 DKK). Features: Urban camper stop, electricity, water, dump station, close to city center.

⛽ Fuel: **Fuel Stations:** Main chains in Denmark include OK, Circle K, Q8, and Shell. There are no remote stretches without fuel on the main highway from Hirtshals to Copenhagen. **Diesel Price:** Approximately €1.80 - €1.95 per liter (2024-2025 estimates).

🛣️ Tolls: **Tolls:** In Denmark, most roads are toll-free. However, if you cross the Storebælt Bridge (Great Belt Bridge) on the drive from Hirtshals to Copenhagen, there is a toll. For a camper van (under 3500 kg, 6-10m), the cost is approx. 610 DKK (~€82) one way. You can pay with a credit card at the toll booth or use an AutoPASS/Brobizz tag for a discount.

⏰ Timing: **Departure:** Take a morning ferry from Kristiansand (e.g., Fjord Line or Color Line, crossing takes 2h 25m to 3h 15m) to Hirtshals, Denmark. **Arrival:** Drive from Hirtshals to Copenhagen (~4.5 hours). Aim to arrive in Copenhagen by late afternoon to settle into the campsite and perhaps take an evening stroll or visit Tivoli Gardens (open late).

🛒 Supermarkets: **Supermarkets:** Main chains in Denmark include REMA 1000, Netto, Lidl, Føtex, and Coop 365. REMA 1000 and Netto are excellent budget-friendly options and are widely available along the route and near campsites in Copenhagen.

🧺 Laundry: **The Laundromat Cafe** (Elmegade 15, 2200 København N) is a popular spot where you can do self-service laundry while enjoying a coffee or meal. Alternatively, most major campsites like DCU-Camping Absalon have on-site laundry facilities.

💧 Water/Dump: Most campsites in Copenhagen (like DCU-Camping Absalon or Charlottenlund Fort) offer dedicated camper service areas for fresh water fill and grey/black water dump. If wild camping, you can often find service points at larger gas stations or use the facilities at paid camper stops like Camperparking.dk Copenhagen.

🏥 Safety: **Emergency Number:** 112 for life-threatening emergencies. For non-life-threatening medical help in the Copenhagen area, call 1813. **Nearest Hospital:** Rigshospitalet (Blegdamsvej 9, 2100 København). **Warnings:** Be extremely mindful of cyclists in Copenhagen; they have the right of way and bike lanes are very busy. Ensure your camper meets the environmental zone requirements if driving into the city center.

💰 Daily budget: €180-250 (Ferry: ~€100-150 depending on booking time, Campsite: ~€40-60, Food/Groceries: ~€40-60, Activities/Transport: ~€20-40)

🅿️ Accommodation: Camping des Cygnes / Aire de Camping-Car des Cygnes. 📍 Maps (49°55'15.7"N 2°15'36.1"E). Price: ~€20-25/night. Features: Electricity, water, grey/black water disposal, WiFi, playground, close to Amiens center.

⛽ Fuel: Main chains in Germany: Aral, Shell, Esso, Total. Main chains in France: TotalEnergies, Esso, and supermarket stations (Carrefour, Leclerc, Super U) which are usually cheaper. No major remote stretches without fuel. Approximate diesel price: €1.90 - €1.98 per liter (France/Germany average).

🛣️ Tolls: The route from Bremen to Amiens via the Netherlands and Belgium is mostly toll-free. In France, some autoroutes have tolls (péage), but you can easily avoid them on this specific route by taking toll-free highways or national roads. If using toll roads in France, expect around €10-€20 for a camper van (Class 2). No vignette required for Germany, Netherlands, or Belgium for standard camper vans.

⏰ Timing: Depart Bremen around 08:30. The drive is approximately 6.5 to 7.5 hours (around 570 km). Expected arrival in Amiens around 16:00, allowing time for breaks. Time-sensitive: Check-in at the campsite before reception closes (usually around 19:00).

🛒 Supermarkets: Carrefour Market (22 bis Rue du Général Leclerc, Amiens), Super U, Leclerc, and Auchan. Supermarkets are plentiful along the route in Germany, Netherlands, Belgium, and France.

🧺 Laundry: Espace Laverie (64 Rue Saint Leu, 80000 Amiens) or Wash.ME at Super U Amiens.

💧 Water/Dump: Available at Camping des Cygnes (grey/black water disposal and fresh water refill). There is also a service point at the Aire de camping-car à la ferme de Picquigny.

🏥 Safety: Nearest hospital: CHU Amiens-Picardie (Centre Hospitalier Universitaire), 1 Rond-Point du Professeur Christian Cabrol, 80054 Amiens. Emergency numbers: 112 (General EU emergency), 15 (Ambulance/SAMU), 17 (Police), 18 (Fire). Warnings: Watch out for narrow streets in the historic center of Amiens.

💰 Daily budget: €130-160 (Campsite: €20-30, Fuel: €50-70, Tolls: €0-10, Food/Activities: €60-80)

⛽ Fuel: Main chains: TotalEnergies, BP, Esso, and supermarket stations (Leclerc, Carrefour, Intermarché) which are usually cheaper. No remote stretches without fuel on this major autoroute route. Diesel price: ~€1.75 - €1.85 per liter (supermarket stations) to ~€2.10 (autoroute stations).

🛣️ Tolls: France uses a toll booth system (Péage) on Autoroutes. A camper van (usually Class 2) will cost roughly €0.16-€0.17 per km. The route from Amiens to Amboise via A16/A10 will cost approximately €45-€55 in tolls. Payment by card or cash at booths, or via a Télépéage tag (like Bip&Go).

⏰ Timing: Suggest departing Amiens around 09:00. The drive is about 370 km (approx. 4 hours). Expected arrival in Amboise around 13:30 (allowing for a rest stop). Afternoon: Visit Clos Lucé (check closing times, usually 18:00 or 19:00 in summer).

🛒 Supermarkets: Main chains in France: E.Leclerc, Carrefour, Super U, Intermarché, Auchan, Lidl, Aldi. In Amboise, there is a large E.Leclerc and an Intermarché Super easily accessible for stocking up before heading to the campsite.

🧺 Laundry: Self-service laundry available in Amboise town center (e.g., Laverie Automatique Amboise, near the main supermarket areas). Alternatively, check if the campsite has washing machines.

💧 Water/Dump: Available at Aire CAMPING-CAR PARK d'Amboise (water fill and grey/black water dump included in the price). Dedicated service point on site.

🏥 Safety: Nearest hospital: Centre Hospitalier Intercommunal Amboise/Château-Renault (Rue des Ursulines, Amboise). Emergency number: 112 (European standard) or 15 (SAMU/Medical). Warnings: Watch for narrow streets in the historic center of Amboise; stick to main roads with the camper.

💰 Daily budget: €120-150

D41 · 06/08 · Amiens → Loire 🇫🇷

Galette complète take-away ~€8. Picnic on the Loire banks! Market: Marché d'Amboise (Place du Marché) — rillettes, Sainte-Maure goat cheeses, fruit. Fri and Sun morning. Tip: Vouvray in cellar ~€5-8!

🛴 Scooters: Loire à Vélo bike lanes, perfect along the castles → see rentals 🚴 Bike rental: Détours de Loire (~€15-25/day, kids bikes available) → see rentals

Maps: 📍 Amboise

👶 Kids: 1. Château du Clos Lucé (Amboise): Features life-sized, interactive models of Leonardo da Vinci's inventions in the park. 2. Parc des Mini-Châteaux (Amboise): A park with miniature versions of the Loire castles. 3. Renting bikes for a flat, easy family ride along the "Loire à Vélo" cycle paths.

📋 Practical Info

🅿️ Accommodation: 1. Camping l'Ile d'Or (Amboise) - 📍 Maps Price: ~€25-35/night. Features: electricity, water, WiFi, playground, pool, view of the castle. 2. Aire de camping-car Chambord - 📍 Maps Price: ~€11/night. Features: parking, water, dump station, walking distance to Château de Chambord.

⛽ Fuel: Main chains: TotalEnergies, Esso, Shell. Supermarket stations (E.Leclerc, Carrefour, Intermarché) are significantly cheaper. No remote stretches without fuel in this region. Approximate diesel price: €1.90 - €2.15 per liter.

🛣️ Tolls: Pay-per-use toll booths (péage) on autoroutes (e.g., A10, A85). Camper vans are usually Class 2 (higher rate than cars). However, driving between castles is mostly on free departmental roads (D-roads). Approximate cost: €0 - €15 depending on autoroute usage.

⏰ Timing: Suggested departure: 08:30 AM to arrive at the first castle by opening time (usually 09:00 or 09:30 AM) to avoid peak summer crowds. Time-sensitive: Castles close around 18:00-19:00 in August. Pre-booking tickets online is highly recommended to skip queues.

🛒 Supermarkets: Main chains: E.Leclerc, Carrefour, Super U, Intermarché, Auchan. Easily found on the outskirts of towns like Amboise, Blois, and Tours.

🧺 Laundry: Available inside major campsites like Camping l'Ile d'Or. Alternatively, look for 24/7 outdoor self-service kiosks (e.g., Revolution Laundry) located in supermarket parking lots (Super U, Intermarché).

💧 Water/Dump: Fresh water fill and grey/black water dump are available at most campsites and dedicated Aires de camping-car. Municipal service points (Flot Bleu or similar) often require a token (jeton) or credit card for fresh water (~€2-3), while dumping is typically free.

🏥 Safety: Nearest hospitals: CHRU de Tours (Tours) or Centre Hospitalier de Blois. Emergency numbers: 112 (General), 15 (Medical), 17 (Police). Warnings: Watch for cyclists on shared roads. Be aware of height barriers (barrières de hauteur) at some standard parking lots; always follow signs for dedicated camper/bus parking at the castles.

💰 Daily budget: €170-190

D42 · 07/08 · Loire Castles 🇫🇷

Requires daily fishing license (~€15) at cartedepeche.fr. Children <12 free. 🌭 Lunch: galette complète (savory crepe with ham-cheese-egg, ~€7). Kids snack: pain au chocolat from the bakery

Maps: 📍 Clos Lucé

👶 Kids: San Sebastian is very kid-friendly. Recommended activities include taking the funicular up to Monte Igueldo to visit the vintage amusement park with great views, or visiting the San Sebastian Aquarium. The beaches (like Ondarreta) are also great for families.

📋 Practical Info

🅿️ Accommodation: Area Autocaravanas Donosti (Berio) | GPS: 43.3079, -2.0143 | Price: ~€12/night (summer rate) | Features: 44 pitches, water fill/dump, close to bus stop and bike paths to city center. Note: Max stay 72 hours, no awnings/chairs allowed outside.

⛽ Fuel: Main fuel chains in France include TotalEnergies, BP, and supermarket stations (Leclerc, Carrefour) which are usually cheaper. In Spain, Repsol and Cepsa are common. Diesel in Spain is generally cheaper than in France (approx. €1.45/L in Spain vs higher in France). It is recommended to refuel once crossing into Spain. No major remote stretches without fuel on this main highway route.

🛣️ Tolls: The route from the Loire Valley to San Sebastian primarily uses the French autoroute network (A10 and A63). France uses a toll booth system (péage) where you pay by distance. A camper van (usually Class 2) will cost approximately €60-€80 in tolls for this stretch. Spain's AP-8 near the border also has a small toll.

⏰ Timing: Depart the Loire region in the morning (around 8:30 AM) to allow for the long drive (approx. 5-6 hours depending on exact starting point). Aim to arrive in San Sebastian by mid-afternoon (3:00 PM - 4:00 PM) to secure a spot at the popular Berio camper area, as it fills up quickly in summer.

🛒 Supermarkets: In France, Leclerc and Carrefour are common along the route. Near the border (e.g., Irún/Hendaye), there are large supermarkets. In San Sebastian, Eroski, Super Amara, and Lidl are popular. There is an Eroski and a Lidl accessible for groceries.

🧺 Laundry: Self-service laundries are available in San Sebastian, such as 'Lavanderia Wash & Dry' or 'Speed Queen' locations in the city center.

💧 Water/Dump: Water fill and dump services are available at the Area Autocaravanas Donosti (Berio) in San Sebastian. The service is free of charge for those staying at the camper area.

🏥 Safety: Nearest hospital: Hospital Universitario Donostia (Paseo Dr. Beguiristain, s/n, 20014 Donostia-San Sebastian). Emergency number in Spain is 112. Warning: The camper area in Berio can be tight for very large motorhomes, and summer traffic near the border can be heavy.

💰 Daily budget: €110-140 (Campsite: €12, Fuel/Tolls: €40-50, Food/Supermarket: €40-50, Activities/Misc: €20-30)

D43 · 08/08 · Loire → San Sebastián 🇫🇷→🇪🇸

Bocadillo de tortilla from bars ~€4-6. Pintxos tour = ~€15/person to be full! Market: Mercado de la Bretxa (Aldamar Kalea) — fish, Basque cheeses. D43 = Saturday → AVAILABLE! — 📍 Maps 🌲 Playa de la Zurriola — surfing and sunset ➕ alt: La Perla — thalassotherapy on La Concha → see ♨️ details 🎣 Fishing: San Sebastián harbor pier or Igueldo cliffs — seabream, mackerel, gilt-head bream. ⚠️ Requires recreational sea fishing license (valid throughout Spain, ~€43/3 years online).

👶 Kids: 1. Take a photo with the giant floral 'Puppy' outside the Guggenheim Museum. 2. Ride the Funicular de Artxanda for great views and a fun experience for kids. 3. Visit Doña Casilda Iturrizar Park, which has a great playground, ducks, and plenty of space to run around.

📋 Practical Info

🅿️ Accommodation: Area de Autocaravanas Kobetamendi (Bilbao). GPS: 43.2596, -2.9635. Price: ~€15-20 per night. Key features: Electricity, fresh water, grey/black water dump, stunning views over Bilbao, and a direct bus line (58) to the city center right outside the gate. Very popular, arrive early.

⛽ Fuel: Main fuel station chains in the Basque Country include Repsol, Cepsa, Petronor, and Avia. The route is well-populated with no remote stretches. Approximate diesel price is €1.65 - €1.72 per liter.

🛣️ Tolls: The AP-8 highway from San Sebastián to Bilbao is a toll road. The toll system uses traditional toll booths (cash/card accepted) or Via-T electronic tags. Approximate cost for a camper van is around €13-€18 depending on the exact vehicle classification.

⏰ Timing: Suggest departing San Sebastián around 09:30 to arrive in Bilbao by 11:00. Park the camper at Kobetamendi and take the bus (line 58) into the city. If visiting the Guggenheim Museum, book tickets in advance (opens at 10:00, closed on some Mondays).

🛒 Supermarkets: Main supermarket chains in the Basque Country are Eroski (very common local chain), Mercadona, and BM Supermercados. There are large Eroski hypermarkets along the route and smaller supermarkets in Bilbao for daily needs.

🧺 Laundry: Speed Queen or Colada Expres self-service laundries are available in Bilbao city center if needed, though it's best to do laundry while parked and take public transport into the city.

💧 Water/Dump: Full service (fresh water fill, grey/black water dump) available at Area de Autocaravanas Kobetamendi. Dedicated service point included in the overnight price.

🏥 Safety: Nearest hospital: Hospital Universitario Basurto (Bilbao). Emergency number: 112. Warnings: Avoid driving the camper van into Bilbao's city center or Casco Viejo (Old Town) due to narrow streets and limited parking; use the camper area on the outskirts and rely on public transport.

💰 Daily budget: €130-160

GPS: 43.1533, -4.6369

Camping Naranjo de Bulnes (Arenas de Cabrales, Asturias)
GPS: 43.3056, -4.8142
Price: ~€35-45/night
Features: Electricity, water, WiFi, playground, riverside location.

⛽ Fuel: Main chains: Repsol, Cepsa, BP, Petronor. Diesel price: ~€1.45-1.55/L. Note: Fill up in Bilbao or along the A-8 coast before heading inland into the Picos de Europa mountains, as mountain stations are sparse.

💧 Water/Dump: Fresh water fill and grey/black water dump are available at recommended campsites (La Viorna, Naranjo de Bulnes). Dedicated motorhome areas (Áreas de Autocaravanas) in towns like Cangas de Onís also offer service points.

Warnings: Mountain roads (N-621 through Desfiladero de la Hermida) are very narrow, winding, and have overhanging rocks. Drive the camper van with extreme caution and yield to larger vehicles.
